<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-
autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">HUGOTON 
ROYALTY TRUST</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><a 
name="GlossaryOfTerms_064212"></a><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">GLOSSARY OF TERMS</font></u></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">HUGOTON 
ROYALTY TRUST</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><a 
name="PartiFinancialInformation_064216"></a><u><font size="2" face="Times New 
Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">PART&nbsp;I
- - FINANCIAL INFORMATION</font></u></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><a
name="Item1_FinancialStatements__064217"></a><i><font size="2" face="Times New 
Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Item 1.&#160; Financial
Statements.</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
condensed financial statements included herein are presented, without audit,
pursuant to the rules&nbsp;and regulations of the Securities and Exchange
Commission.&#160; Certain information and
footnote disclosures normally included in annual financial statements have been
condensed or omitted pursuant to such rules&nbsp;and regulations, although the
trustee believes that the disclosures are adequate to make the information
presented not misleading.&#160; These
condensed financial statements should be read in conjunction with the 
trust&#146;s
financial statements and the notes thereto included in the trust&#146;s Annual
Report on Form&nbsp;10-K.&#160; In the opinion
of the trustee, all adjustments, consisting only of normal recurring
adjustments, necessary to present fairly the assets, liabilities and trust
corpus of the Hugoton Royalty Trust at September&nbsp;30, 2005 and the
distributable income and changes in trust corpus for the three- and nine-month
periods ended September&nbsp;30, 2005 and 2004 have been included.&#160; 
Distributable income for such interim periods
is not necessarily indicative of the distributable income for the full 
year.</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-
autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-
autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-
autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><a 
name="ReportOfIndependentRegisteredPubl_064221"></a><b><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">REPORT OF 
INDEPENDENT REGISTERED PUBLIC ACCOUNTING FIRM</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .1in;text-autospace:none;text-
indent:-.1in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-
size:10.0pt;">Bank of America, N.A., as Trustee<br>
for the Hugoton Royalty Trust:</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We
have reviewed the accompanying condensed statement of assets, liabilities and
trust corpus of the Hugoton Royalty Trust as of September&nbsp;30, 2005 and the
related condensed statements of distributable income and changes in trust
corpus for the three- and nine-month periods ended September&nbsp;30, 2005 and
2004.&#160; These condensed financial
statements are the responsibility of the trustee.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We
conducted our review in accordance with standards established by the Public
Company Accounting Oversight Board (United States).&#160; A review of interim 
financial information
consists principally of applying analytical procedures to financial data and 
making
inquiries of persons responsible for financial and accounting matters.&#160; It 
is substantially less in scope than an
audit conducted in accordance with the standards of the Public Company
Accounting Oversight Board (United States), the objective of which is the
expression of an opinion regarding the financial statements taken as a
whole.&#160; Accordingly, we do not express
such an opinion.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
accompanying condensed financial statements are prepared on a modified cash
basis as described in Note&nbsp;1 which is a comprehensive basis of accounting
other than accounting principles generally accepted in the United States of
America.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Based
on our review, we are not aware of any material modifications that should be
made to the condensed financial statements referred to above for them to be in
conformity with the basis of accounting described in Note&nbsp;1.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We
have previously audited, in accordance with the standards of the Public Company
Accounting Oversight Board (United States), the statement of assets,
liabilities and trust corpus of the Hugoton Royalty Trust as of 
December&nbsp;31,
2004, and the related statements of distributable income and changes in trust
corpus for the year then ended (not presented herein), included in the 
trust&#146;s
2004 Annual Report on Form&nbsp;10-K, and in our report dated March&nbsp;14,
2005, we expressed an unqualified opinion on those financial statements.&#160; 
In our opinion, the information set forth in
the accompanying condensed statement of assets, liabilities and trust corpus as
of December&nbsp;31, 2004 is fairly stated, in all material respects, in
relation to the statement of assets, liabilities and trust corpus included in
the trust&#146;s 2004 Annual Report on Form&nbsp;10-K from which it has been
derived.</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-
autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">HUGOTON 
ROYALTY TRUST</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><a 
name="NotesToCondensedFinancialStatemen_064238"></a><b><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Notes to 
Condensed Financial Statements </font></b>(Unaudited)</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-
autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">1.</font></b><b><font size="1" 
style="font-size:3.0pt;font-
weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
&#160;&#160; </font></b><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Basis of 
Accounting</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
financial statements of Hugoton Royalty Trust are prepared on the following
basis and are not intended to present financial position and results of
operations in conformity with generally accepted accounting principles 
(&#147;GAAP&#148;):</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 15.1pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 45.35pt;text-
autospace:none;text-indent:-15.15pt;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160; </font>Net profits income recorded for a month is
the amount computed and paid by XTO Energy Inc., the owner of the underlying
properties, to Bank of America, N.A., as trustee for the trust.&#160; Net 
profits income consists of net proceeds
received by XTO Energy Inc. from the underlying properties in the prior month,
multiplied by a net profits percentage of 80%.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 45.35pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-
15.15pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 45.35pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Costs
deducted in the calculation of net proceeds for the 80% net profits interests
generally include applicable taxes, transportation, marketing and legal costs,
production expense, development costs, operating charges and other 
costs.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 45.35pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 45.35pt;text-
autospace:none;text-indent:-15.15pt;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160; </font>Net profits income is computed separately for
each of three conveyances under which the net profits interests were conveyed
to the trust.&#160; If monthly costs exceed
revenues for any conveyance, such excess costs must be recovered, with accrued
interest, from future net proceeds of that conveyance and cannot reduce net
proceeds from the other conveyances.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 45.35pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-
15.15pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 45.35pt;text-
autospace:none;text-indent:-15.15pt;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160; </font>Trust expenses are recorded based on
liabilities paid and cash reserves established by the trustee for liabilities
and contingencies.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 45.35pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-
15.15pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 45.35pt;text-
autospace:none;text-indent:-15.15pt;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman"
style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160; </font>Distributions to unitholders are recorded
when declared by the trustee.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 45.35pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-
15.15pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
trust&#146;s financial statements differ from those prepared in conformity with 
GAAP
because revenues are recognized when received rather than accrued in the month
of production, expenses are recognized when paid rather than when incurred and
certain cash reserves may be established by the trustee for contingencies which
would not be recorded under GAAP.&#160; This
comprehensive basis of accounting other than GAAP corresponds to the accounting
permitted for royalty trusts by the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission, as
specified by Staff Accounting Bulletin Topic 12:E, Financial Statements of
Royalty Trusts.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 15.1pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Most
accounting pronouncements apply to entities whose financial statements are
prepared in accordance with GAAP, directing such entities to accrue or defer
revenues and expenses in a period other than when such revenues were received
or expenses were paid.&#160; Because the trust&#146;s
financial statements are prepared on the modified cash basis, as described
above, most accounting pronouncements are not applicable to the trust&#146;s
financial statements.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
initial carrying value of the net profits interests of $247,066,951 represents
XTO Energy Inc.&#146;s historical net book value for the interests on 
December&nbsp;1,
1998, the date of the transfer to the trust.&#160;
Amortization of the net profits interests is calculated on a unit-of-production
basis and charged directly to trust corpus.&#160;
Accumulated amortization was $72,582,285 as of September&nbsp;30, 2005
and $64,515,137 as of December&nbsp;31, 2004.</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-
autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-
autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-
size:10.0pt;">10</font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">
<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">
</font></div>
</div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 15.1pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
monthly development deduction was $2 million in January&nbsp;2005; it has been
increased three times during 2005 as a result of increased development activity
and higher costs.&#160; The deductions were
increased to $2.4 million beginning with the February distribution, to $3.3
million beginning with the July&nbsp;distribution and to $5.1 million beginning
with the October&nbsp;distribution.&#160; XTO
Energy Inc. has advised the trustee that it currently expects the monthly
deduction will remain at $5.1 million for the remainder of 2005, subject to
reevaluation and revision as necessary.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 15.1pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-
autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">3.</font></b><b><font size="1" 
style="font-size:3.0pt;font-
weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
&#160;&#160; </font></b><b><font style="font-
weight:bold;">Contingencies</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-
style:italic;">Litigation</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:15.1pt;"><font 
size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">XTO
Energy Inc. is a defendant in lawsuits related to the underlying properties
that could, if adversely determined, decrease future trust distributable income
attributable to production on or after December&nbsp;1, 1998, the creation date
of the trust.&#160; Any damages relating to
production prior to December&nbsp;1, 1998 will be borne by XTO Energy 
Inc.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 15.1pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On
October&nbsp;17, 1997, an action, styled <i><font style="font-
style:italic;">United
States of America ex rel. Grynberg v. Cross Timbers Oil Company, et
al.</font></i>,
was filed in the United States District Court for the Western District of
Oklahoma by Jack J. Grynberg on behalf of the United States under the <i><font 
style="font-style:italic;">qui tam</font></i> provisions of the U.S. False
Claims Act against XTO Energy Inc.&#160; The
plaintiff alleges that XTO Energy Inc. underpaid royalties on natural gas
produced from federal leases and lands owned by Native Americans in amounts in
excess of 20% as a result of mismeasuring the volume of natural gas,
incorrectly analyzing its heating content and improperly valuing the natural gas
during at least the past ten years.&#160; The
plaintiff seeks treble damages for the unpaid royalties (with interest,
attorneys&#146; fees and expenses), civil penalties between $5,000 and $10,000 
for
each violation of the U.S. False Claims Act, and an order for XTO Energy Inc.
to cease the allegedly improper measuring practices.&#160; This lawsuit against 
XTO Energy Inc. and
similar lawsuits filed by Grynberg against more than 300 other companies have
been consolidated in the United States District Court for Wyoming.&#160; In 
October&nbsp;2002, the court granted a
motion to dismiss Grynberg&#146;s royalty valuation claims, and Grynberg&#146;s 
appeal of
this decision was dismissed for lack of appellate jurisdiction in 
May&nbsp;2003.&#160; The parties have completed discovery
regarding whether the plaintiff has met the jurisdictional prerequisites for
maintaining an action under the U.S. False Claims Act.&#160; In June&nbsp;2004, 
XTO Energy Inc. joined
with other defendants in filing a motion to dismiss, contending that the
plaintiff has not satisfied the jurisdictional requirements to maintain this
action.&#160; A hearing on this motion
occurred in March&nbsp;2005, and in May&nbsp;2005, the special master, who was
appointed by the district judge to expedite matters and</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-
autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-
autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-
size:10.0pt;">11</font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">
<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">
</font></div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-
autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">make
recommendations to the district judge in the case, issued a report and
recommendation to dismiss the case against some defendants but to retain
jurisdiction of the case involving XTO Energy Inc. and other defendants.&#160;
XTO Energy Inc. and other defendants filed a
motion to modify the special master&#146;s report, requesting the district judge
to
also dismiss the case as to XTO Energy Inc. and other defendants.&#160; While 
XTO Energy Inc. is unable to predict
the outcome of this case or estimate the amount of any possible loss, it has
informed the trustee that it believes that the allegations of this lawsuit are
without merit and intends to vigorously defend the action.&#160; However, an 
order to change measuring
practices or a related settlement could adversely affect the trust by reducing
net proceeds in the future by an amount that is presently not determinable,
but, in XTO Energy Inc. management&#146;s opinion, is not currently expected to 
be
material to the trust&#146;s annual distributable income, financial position or
liquidity.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 15.1pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Certain
of the underlying properties are involved in various other lawsuits and certain
governmental proceedings arising in the ordinary course of business. XTO Energy
Inc. has advised the trustee that it does not believe that the ultimate
resolution of these claims will have a material effect on trust annual
distributable income, financial position or liquidity.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-
style:italic;">Other</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:15.1pt;"><font 
size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Several
states have enacted legislation to require state income tax withholding from
nonresident recipients of oil and gas proceeds.&#160;
After consultation with its state tax counsel, XTO Energy Inc. has
advised the trustee that it believes the trust is not subject to these
withholding requirements.&#160; However,
regulations are subject to change by the various states, which could change
this conclusion.&#160; In the event it is
determined that the trust is required to withhold state taxes, distributions to
the unitholders would be reduced by the required amount, subject to the
unitholder&#146;s right to file a state tax return to claim any refund 
due.</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-
autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-
autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-
size:10.0pt;">12</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-
autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><a 
name="Item2_TrusteesDiscussionAndAnalys_064245"></a><i><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Item 2.&#160;
Trustee&#146;s
Discussion and Analysis.</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
following discussion should be read in conjunction with the trustee&#146;s
discussion and analysis contained in the trust&#146;s 2004 annual report, as 
well as
the condensed financial statements and notes thereto included in this quarterly
report on Form&nbsp;10-Q.&#160; The trust&#146;s
Annual Report on Form&nbsp;10-K, quarterly reports on Form&nbsp;10-Q, current
reports on Form&nbsp;8-K and all amendments to those reports are available on
the trust&#146;s web site at www.hugotontrust.com.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Distributable 
Income</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-
style:italic;">Quarter</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For
the quarter ended September&nbsp;30, 2005, net profits income was $24,325,921,
as compared to $23,521,511 for third quarter 2004.&#160; This 3% increase in net
profits income is
primarily the result of higher oil and gas prices.&#160; See &#147;Net Profits 
Income&#148; on the following
page.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2"
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">After
adding interest income of $29,600 and deducting administration expense of
$51,321, distributable income for the quarter ended September&nbsp;30, 2005 was
$24,304,200, or $0.607605 per unit of beneficial interest.&#160; Administration 
expense for the quarter
decreased 50% from the prior year quarter primarily because of the timing of
expenditures.&#160; For third quarter 2004,
distributable income was $23,428,840 or $0.585721 per unit.&#160; Distributions 
to unitholders for the quarter
ended September&nbsp;30, 2005 were:</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Nine 
Months</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For
the nine months ended September&nbsp;30, 2005, net profits income was
$73,110,521, compared with $60,868,299 for the same 2004 period.&#160; This 20% 
increase in net profits income is
primarily the result of higher oil and gas prices.&#160; See &#147;Net Profits 
Income&#148; on the following
page.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">After
adding interest income of $71,509 and deducting administration expense of
$347,630, distributable income for the nine months ended September&nbsp;30,
2005 was $72,834,400, or $1.820860&#160; per
unit of beneficial interest.&#160;
Administration expense for the first nine months of 2005 was 14% higher
than in the first nine months of 2004 primarily because of fees related to the
audit of the trust&#146;s internal control over financial reporting for 2004 and
the
timing of expenditures.&#160; For the nine
months ended September&nbsp;30, 2004, distributable income was $60,584,160 or
$1.514604 per unit.</font></p>

autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-
size:10.0pt;">13</font></p>

face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-
autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2"
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Net Profits 
Income</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Net
profits income is recorded when received by the trust, which is the month
following receipt by XTO Energy Inc., and generally two months after oil and
gas production.&#160; Net profits income is
generally affected by three major factors:</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 30.2pt;text-
autospace:none;text-indent:-15.1pt;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160; </font>oil and gas sales volumes,</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 30.2pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-
15.1pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 30.2pt;text-
autospace:none;text-indent:-15.1pt;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160; </font>oil and gas sales prices, and</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 30.2pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-
15.1pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 30.2pt;text-
autospace:none;text-indent:-15.1pt;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160; </font>costs deducted in the calculation of net
profits income.</p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-
autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-
autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-
size:10.0pt;">14</font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">
<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">
</font></div>
</div>

  <td width="1%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:1.84%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="1" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">
<hr size="1" width="25%" noshade color="black" align="left">
</font></div>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 9.0pt;text-
autospace:none;text-indent:-9.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Because
of the two-month interval between time of production and receipt of net profits
income by the trust, (1)&nbsp;oil and gas sales for the quarter ended 
September&nbsp;30
generally represent production for the period May&nbsp;through July&nbsp;and 
(2)&nbsp;oil
and gas sales for the nine months ended September&nbsp;30 generally represent
production for the period November&nbsp;through July.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 9.0pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-
9.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 9.0pt;text-
autospace:none;text-indent:-9.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Oil
and gas sales volumes are allocated to the net profits interests based upon a
formula that considers oil and gas prices and the total amount of production
expense and development costs.&#160; Changes
in any of these factors may result in disproportionate fluctuations in volumes
allocated to the net profits interests.&#160;
Therefore, comparative discussion of oil and gas sales volumes is based
on the underlying properties.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 9.0pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-
9.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 9.0pt;text-
autospace:none;text-indent:-9.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)</font><font size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>See
Note 2 to Condensed Financial Statements.</p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-
autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
following are explanations of significant variances on the underlying
properties from third quarter 2004 to third quarter 2005 and from the first
nine months of 2004 to the comparable period in 2005:</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Sales 
Volumes</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-
style:italic;">Gas</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2"
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Third
quarter gas sales volumes remained relatively unchanged as increased production
from new wells and workovers and the timing of cash receipts was offset by
natural production decline.&#160; Gas sales
volumes for the nine-month period decreased 2% primarily because of natural
production decline and the timing of cash receipts, partially offset by
increased production from new wells and workovers.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-
style:italic;">Oil</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Oil
sales volumes increased 4% for the third quarter and 2% for the nine-month
period primarily because of increased production from new wells and workovers
and the timing of cash receipts, partially offset by natural production
decline.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">See
&#147;Gulf of Mexico Hurricanes&#148; below.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Sales 
Prices</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-
style:italic;">Gas</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
third quarter 2005 average gas price was $6.17 per Mcf, a 12% increase from the
third quarter 2004 average gas price of $5.50 per Mcf.&#160; For the nine-month 
period, the average gas
price increased 23% to $6.09 per Mcf in 2005 from $4.96 per Mcf in 2004.&#160; 
Gas prices increased for the third quarter
and for the nine-month period primarily because of increased demand,
warmer-than-normal temperatures and reduced gas production as a result of 
July&nbsp;tropical
storms in the Gulf of Mexico.&#160; Prices
will continue to be affected by weather, the U.S. economy, the level of North
American production, crude oil prices and import levels of liquified natural
gas, and are expected to remain volatile.&#160;
The third quarter 2005 gas price is primarily related to production from
May&nbsp;through July&nbsp;2005, when the average NYMEX price was $7.08 per
MMBtu, or 13% higher than the comparable 2004 period average NYMEX price of
$6.25 per MMBtu.&#160; The average NYMEX price
for August&nbsp;and September&nbsp;2005 was $10.68 per MMBtu.&#160; At 
October&nbsp;21, 2005, the average NYMEX
futures price for the following twelve months was $11.58 per MMBtu.&#160; The 
trust gas price for August 2005
production, included in the October 2005 distribution, was $1.05 per Mcf lower
than the NYMEX price.&#160; This decrement is
expected to widen for September and October production, which will affect the
November and December 2005 distributions.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-
style:italic;">Oil</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
third quarter 2005 average oil price was $52.49 per Bbl, a 36% increase from
the third quarter 2004 average oil price of $38.59 per Bbl.&#160; The year-to-
date average oil price increased
40% to $49.49 per Bbl in 2005 from $35.30 per Bbl in 2004.&#160; Oil prices 
increased for the third quarter
and for the nine-month period primarily because of increasing global demand and
supply shortage concerns, inadequate refining capacity, reduced production as a
result of July&nbsp;tropical storms in the Gulf of Mexico, market speculation
and political instability, and are expected to remain volatile.&#160; Oil prices
increased to record levels in August&nbsp;2005,
exceeding $69.00 per Bbl.&#160; The average
NYMEX price for August&nbsp;and September&nbsp;2005 was $65.22 per Bbl.&#160; At
October&nbsp;21, 2005, the average NYMEX
futures price for the following twelve months was $61.12 per Bbl.&#160; Recent 
trust oil prices have averaged
approximately $2.40 per Bbl lower than the NYMEX price.</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-
autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-
autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-
size:10.0pt;">16</font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">
<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">

<div>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-
autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">See
&#147;Gulf of Mexico Hurricanes&#148; below.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-
weight:bold;">Costs</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-
style:italic;">Taxes</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Taxes,
transportation and other increased 21% for the quarter and 31% for the
nine-month period primarily because of increased production taxes related to
higher revenues.&#160; The increase for the
nine-month period was also affected by property taxes related to the timing of
cash disbursements.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-
style:italic;">Production</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Production
expense increased 2% for the quarter and decreased 2% for the nine-month
period.&#160; Fluctuations in production
expense are primarily because of the timing of maintenance projects as well as
the timing of cash disbursements.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-
style:italic;">Development</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2"
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Development
costs deducted in the calculation of net profits income are based on the
development budget.&#160; These development
costs increased 94% for the third quarter and 56% for the nine-month period
primarily because of increased development activity in western Oklahoma and
higher drilling costs in 2005.&#160; During
the first nine months of 2005, 24 wells were completed and four wells were
pending completion on the underlying properties at September&nbsp;30.&#160; XTO 
Energy Inc. has informed the trustee that
it plans to drill 37 wells and perform approximately 25 workovers and 65
restimulations during 2005.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As
of December&nbsp;31, 2004, cumulative actual development costs exceeded
cumulative budgeted costs deducted by $319,927.&#160;
In calculating net profits income, XTO Energy Inc. deducted budgeted
costs of $9.9 million for the quarter and $23.9 million for the nine-month
period.&#160; After considering actual costs
of $10.9 million for the quarter and $25.5 million for the nine-month period,
cumulative actual costs exceeded cumulative budgeted costs deducted by $1.9 
million
at September&nbsp;30, 2005.&#160; See
Note&nbsp;2 to Condensed Financial Statements.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Because
of increased development activity and higher costs, the monthly development
cost deduction was increased from $2.4 million to $3.3 million beginning with
the July&nbsp;2005 distribution and to $5.1 million beginning with the 
October&nbsp;2005
distribution.&#160; Development projects have
recently been accelerated because of gas supply disruptions and higher
prices.&#160; XTO Energy Inc. has advised the
trustee that it currently expects the monthly development cost deduction will
remain at $5.1 million for the remainder of 2005, subject to reevaluation and
revision as necessary.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-
style:italic;">Overhead</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Overhead
decreased 3% for the quarter and increased 2% for the nine-month period.&#160; 
Decreased overhead for the quarter is
primarily because of the timing of an annual Oklahoma administrative fee.&#160; 
Increased overhead for the nine-month period
is primarily because of the annual rate adjustment based on an industry 
index.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2"
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Gulf of Mexico
Hurricanes</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In
late August&nbsp;and September&nbsp;2005, hurricanes in the Gulf of Mexico
disrupted a significant portion of U.S. oil and gas production, leading to
higher prices.&#160; These increased prices
will affect distributions to unitholders beginning with the November&nbsp;2005
distribution to be paid in December&nbsp;2005.&#160;
The underlying</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-
autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-
autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-
size:10.0pt;">17</font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-
autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">properties
to the trust are not located near the Gulf and related production was not
significantly affected. However, because of greater supply and weaker demand in
areas where trust related oil and gas is produced, the price received for such
production will be significantly lower than the price received for Gulf 
production
or NYMEX prices.&#160; As a result of storm
damages and related supply shortages, production expense and development costs
are expected to increase throughout the industry.&#160; The duration of these 
higher prices and costs
cannot be predicted.</font></p>

and 15d-15.&#160; Based upon that evaluation,
the trustee concluded that the trust&#146;s disclosure controls and procedures 
are
effective in timely alerting the trustee to material information relating to
the trust required to be included in the trust&#146;s periodic filings with the
Securities and Exchange Commission.&#160; In
its evaluation of disclosure controls and procedures, the trustee has relied,
to the extent considered reasonable, on information provided by XTO Energy
Inc.&#160; There has not been any change in
the trust&#146;s internal control over financial reporting during the period 
covered
by this report that has materially affected, or is reasonably likely to
materially affect, the trust&#146;s internal control over financial 
reporting.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New

Bank of America, N.A. acts as Trustee;</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-

knowledge, this quarterly report does not contain any untrue statement of a

misleading with respect to the period covered by this quarterly report;</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-

knowledge, the financial statements, and other financial information included
in this quarterly report, fairly present in all material respects the financial
condition, distributable income and changes in trust corpus of the registrant as
of, and for, the periods presented in this quarterly report;</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-
indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-

for establishing and maintaining disclosure controls and procedures (as defined
in Exchange Act <br>
Rules&nbsp;13a-15(e)&nbsp;and 15d-15(e)) and internal control over financial
reporting (as defined in Exchange Act Rules&nbsp;13a-15(f)&nbsp;and 15d-15(f)),
or for causing such controls and procedures to be established and maintained,
for the registrant and I have:</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-
indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.2pt;text-indent:-
19.2pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-

</font>Designed such
disclosure controls and procedures, or caused such disclosure controls and
procedures to be designed under my supervision, to ensure that material
information relating to the registrant, including its consolidated
subsidiaries, is made known to me by others within those entities, particularly
during the period in which this report is being prepared;</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.2pt;text-indent:-19.2pt;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.2pt;text-indent:-

</font>Designed such internal

assurance regarding the reliability of financial reporting and the preparation

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.2pt;text-indent:-19.2pt;"><font size="2"

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<body lang="EN-US">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font 
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-
weight:bold;">EXHIBIT&nbsp;32</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New 
Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font 
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-
weight:bold;">Certification
pursuant to 18 U.S.C. Section&nbsp;1350,</font></b></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font 
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">as 
adopted
pursuant to Section&nbsp;906 of the Sarbanes-Oxley Act of 2002</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New 
Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">In
connection with the Quarterly Report of Hugoton Royalty Trust (the 
&#147;Trust&#148;) on Form&nbsp;10-Q
for the quarterly period ended September&nbsp;30, 2005 as filed with the
Securities and Exchange Commission on the date hereof (the &#147;Report&#148;), 
the
undersigned, not in its individual capacity but solely as the trustee of the
Trust, certifies pursuant to 18 U.S.C. Section&nbsp;1350, as adopted pursuant
to Section&nbsp;906 of the Sarbanes-Oxley Act of 2002, that to its 
knowledge:</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New 
Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.25in;"><font 
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(1)</font><font 
size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The
Report fully complies with the requirements of Section&nbsp;13(a)&nbsp;or 
15(d)&nbsp;of
the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended; and</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times 
New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.25in;"><font 
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(2)</font><font 
size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The
information contained in the Report fairly presents, in all material respects,
the financial condition and results of operations of the Trust.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times 
New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" width="100%" style="border-
collapse:collapse;width:100.0%;">
